                   President Hwang Seon-jo of the World Peace Unification Family

1)
Securing the Foundation for Unification
<Prayer> Father, with this one moment, the year 1970 has passed, and now we welcome the new year, new day, and new time of 1971. Please allow the ideal world that you desire to dawn upon us at this moment.
We sincerely thank you for guiding us in carrying out many tasks to ensure that our Unification Church remains an unforgettable year of victory in 1970, and for your efforts to pave the way for the holy path of victory. May the memories left on that path allow us to envision the new year of 1971, and may your unchanging love, guidance, and protection be with us from this morning until the moment we greet 1972.
In this new year, we have the responsibility and mission to prepare all the conditions that we must present before this nation. Therefore, Father, may the entirety of 1971, which begins from this moment, be your year, and may it become a significant and serious year in history for carrying out your will and work.
You already know the tragic fate of this divided Korean Peninsula. After walking the path of suffering for five thousand years, we have yet to escape from it. Father, please have compassion on this nation, which is facing the final barrier at the end of its journey. North and South are separated, unable to come together, longing for each other yet unable to meet, and facing barriers that prevent us from going where we wish. Please have compassion on the fate of this nation. We believe that only you can determine victory and defeat here.
For the future of this nation, for the day of unification of this people, we reflect on how you have chosen and nurtured us, who are insignificant among many. Facing such a historical destiny, we welcome the year 1971.
Here, our hearts must align with your heart, our wishes must align with your will, and our ideals must align with your creative ideals. We only hope for this.
We must become true filial children before you, transcending the history that has not been able to fulfill its duty as loyal subjects. We know that our historical ancestors, who could not fulfill their duty as loyal subjects due to not having a nation you could govern, exist. Father, if there is a path where we can be loyal subjects because there is a nation you can govern, we understand that this path is the rewarding way to fulfill the highest hope of being born as humans. Therefore, please open the way for us to dedicate ourselves entirely to that nation and sovereignty, fulfilling our duty of loyalty and filial piety before you.
We know that from the day humanity's ancestors fell, there has never been a day when you raised up children who could love you and asked them to fulfill your legacy. As we reflect on your longing heart, which has endured throughout the long history, we, your unworthy children, bow before you today, welcoming the new time of the new year. Father, please have compassion on these people.
Their hearts desire to prepare a day of wishes you desire, to embody the image of children who can receive your love and stand in a place where they can love you. They hope to fulfill their duty as loyal subjects before you with one land, one people, and one sovereign nation that you can eternally govern. Father, please know their wishes. In this year of 1971, we must dedicate our lives and everything to ensure that even the land of South Korea is established before your will. Thus, we should be able to draw closer to you. The year 1971 must not flow away like the setting sun; we must not let it pass by without purpose. Please allow us to establish a center to prepare the foundation for your providence and make this a holy year.
Now we welcome the year 1971. We understand that each of our living environments will be different throughout the 365 days of this year. However, even if our living environments are diverse, the path centered on your will must be one. Thus, we must bring about the results of victory. Even if we are in a position of defeat as individuals and in a place of sorrow, we must leave only the results of victory on the path of your will centered on heaven. May we become sons and daughters who pledge victory before your will, dedicating everything, and may we become indispensable absolute figures in fulfilling your will, Father, we sincerely hope and wish for this.
Father, please pour out your love at this time. We long for the original innocent form of Adam and Eve in Eden. We wish to be before you, free of any blemish or flaw, so that when we want to see you, we can see you, and when we want to call you, we can call you, and that we may find a natural place where you can always respond to our requests. Therefore, on this morning, as we take our first step into the new year of 1971, may we embody the image of the beloved children who received your love in the old Eden, able to call you at any time, to rejoice together, to live together, and to act together. We sincerely hope and wish that you will directly govern us within your authority.
Father, we earnestly hope and wish that you will sanctify this morning. We have welcomed this new year many times, yet we still carry the regret of not having welcomed it as a day of your victory, and we know that this remains as your regret. Therefore, in this year of 1971, may it become a year in which we can dedicate all our sincerity and loyalty to the path for your will and welcome a day of victory.
At this time of welcoming the new year, may your hand of blessing be with these people forever, and may your abundant love also be with your children scattered across South Korea. If there are those who long for the headquarters and pray before you at this time, we earnestly hope and wish that you will grant them blessings a million times over.
There are many children abroad who are concerned about your will, longing for Korea and the headquarters as they welcome the new year. Father, we earnestly hope and wish that you will remember them. Although they may be far apart and in different places, may their hearts for you become one, and may their hearts for your will also become one. Thus, may 1971 be a year in which we can bring forth results that will please you and be a year in which your sons and daughters can take pride before all people.
From this year onward, may you personally guide the path we take for the next ten years. This period is indeed a precious time that can determine the fate of the nation. When we look at Korea, who will love this country, who will protect it, and who will save it? We earnestly hope and wish that you will protect, lead, and nurture us to become the warriors who will establish the nation you desire.
We must love this country from the position of loving heaven more than anyone else, and we must love this people and the sovereignty of this nation. We earnestly hope and wish that you will personally govern this entire nation, making it a holy Korea where you can dwell.
May this people become a nation that can be offered to you as your people, and may this land become a territory that can be offered to you as an eternal foundation for victory. We earnestly ask and wish for this.
May you personally lead this entire year that begins from this moment, so that we cannot stray from your providence, and may you personally govern us so that we can pave the way for victory. This is a time to pledge our loyalty and filial piety before you as we joyfully welcome the coming year, so we earnestly ask that you take charge of all our affairs.
Father, please bless all people who welcome the new year, and may you bless the countless saints in the spirit world and the many prophets and ancestors who sacrificed for your will, so that they can further cooperate with the descendants of this land in fulfilling your will. As two thousand years of history have passed since Jesus came to this earth, we earnestly hope and wish that you will grant the special privilege to those who have sacrificed for heaven throughout history to be able to establish an environment for liberation centered around this year and to participate in a free environment where they can welcome you.
May heaven and earth become one to praise the glory of your holy throne, and may your holiness be revealed. We earnestly ask and wish for this. We ask once again that you take charge of everything, and we sincerely pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.
<Words> As we welcome the new year, I sincerely hope that this year will be meaningful for you and that you can fulfill your duty of loyalty and filial piety before God. I also earnestly wish that this year’s journey will be filled with holy purpose and abundant blessings.
The slogan for this year's new beginning is "Securing the Foundation for Unification," as written here (as noted on the blackboard). In other words, we must secure the foundation for unification. This slogan was set with this intention.
12   Securing the Foundation for Unification
The 1970s must lay a solid foundation for itself
Until now, we have set slogans such as "Full-scale Advance" or "Victorious Unification Front" and have been advancing outward, working to create an environment where our will can reach outwards since the 1960s. From 1960 to 1970, we have truly been engaged in a war of attrition. We did not fight for our own interests but rather paid a heavy price to break down the barriers that have stood in the way of our Unification Church.
We did not start from the highest positions in Seoul or the center. When we look at the path we are taking, which is the standard desired by our will, we should have started from the highest standards. However, due to opposition from this people and many churches, we started from the lowest levels and have developed upward until now.
During that period, many individuals sacrificed, and our Unification Church families also endured many sacrifices. We are well aware that many people related to those belonging to the Unification Church in Korea, including relatives and those connected emotionally, suffered because of us.
In any case, we have invested all our efforts for about ten years since 1960 to break down all the barriers of persecution that have arisen externally and to pave the way for victory, aiming for a necessary and appropriate time in this country centered around one goal.
Now, as we enter the 1970s, we believe that from 1971 to 1980, we must lay a solid foundation within ourselves. In other words, rather than fighting against the outside, it is essential for individuals to live a life serving God, families to live a life serving God, churches to live a life serving God, and to establish how to set the standard of serving God centered around this nation and people as a new tradition.
13 
The most important issue in establishing the foundation for unification
Unlike the forms of struggle we have engaged in until now, from now on, we must genuinely establish a relationship with God and deeply root it in our individual selves as well as in our environment. This applies not only to individuals and families but also to churches.
So, what is the core point for unification? This is the question. What standard should we center on for unification, and where should the foundation of that unification be laid? From the perspective of our Unification Church, the foundation must be laid around the church. Before it can be centered around the nation, it must first be centered around the church. However, for the foundation of unification to be established around the church, it must be centered around families that align with the new will. Without establishing this unifying foundation in families, neither the church nor the nation can lay a foundation for unification. Therefore, above all, families are the key issue.
Then, how can we create families that can establish a unifying foundation? We must return to the individual. The issue is that each of us must stand on the foundation of unification. Here, the unifying foundation that each person must establish is...
What is it? The unified foundation that each person should establish was supposed to be set from the Garden of Eden before the fall. In the Garden of Eden, humanity's ancestors, Adam and Eve, were to unite centered on God, and the archangel was to unite centered on those human ancestors. If this had happened, we know well that the archangel could have become one with God centered on Adam and Eve. 

So what is the standard of unity? Ultimately, it is to become one with God, our human ancestors, and the archangel. Therefore, applying this standard to today, unless we secure a victorious foundation within ourselves, the foundation of unity that we desire cannot be formed in families, churches, nations, or the world. This is beyond question. Thus, somehow, my individual self must become one with God. 

The most important issue for us as individuals today is how to establish the standard of becoming one with the archangel after first becoming one with God. When this is disrupted, it is a fact that no matter how well we do everything else, we cannot achieve results aligned with God's will. Therefore, I must raise the standard that humanity's ancestors failed at, centered on myself, and at the same time become one with God, and the archangel must become one centered on me. The question is how this can be achieved.

Here, the archangel represents the angelic world, and 'I' stand in the position of a son who should receive God's love. If the archangel is in the position of a servant, we humans must transcend that servant position and take the position of a son.

God's Desire
So what does God desire regarding the son, and what does He desire regarding the archangel? God hopes for a connection of life that can become one with Him. The reason humanity has not been born as God's sons and daughters centered on His love within His will is due to the fall, and the reason we cannot establish a relationship with God is also due to the fall. Therefore, the most important issue for us today is how I can establish a new connection of life with God.

Failing to establish a connection of life with God and forming a blood relationship centered on the archangel Luciel is the fall. Today, we know that our lives are connected based on such a foundation. Therefore, this life is not the life that God desires. It is not the connection of life that the Creator hoped for. 

We know that it was not the connection that Adam and Eve desired, nor was it the connection that the archangel originally hoped for. In this way, humanity formed a connection of death centered on the archangel, which became the motive for the failure, resulting in our human grief, and God, who could not avoid facing such results, also experienced grief.

Thus, what is God's desire? It is to have people cut off their connection with the world of Satan and establish a connection of life with God, allowing them to return to the original position of Adam and Eve before the fall. This is God's historical desire.

Then, who should be restored first to fulfill this historical desire? Adam must be restored first. However, Adam cannot be restored alone. Since the fall involved both Adam and the archangel, in restoring Adam, we must establish figures in the positions of both the archangel and Adam to find the way back to God. This is the principle of restoration centered on Cain and Abel presented by the Unification Church today.

Restoration cannot happen unless Cain and Abel become one. Cain and Abel must unite under one goal centered on the connection of God's love to return to God; otherwise, we cannot bring liberation to humanity today, achieve personal perfection, or liberate the angelic world.

Therefore, the most pressing issue is how to cut off the connection of life born under the dominion of the archangel Luciel and return to God's side. Adam cannot do this alone; he needs the cooperation of the archangel. In other words, the archangel who has not fallen must help Adam, just as he helped Adam fall, but now he must liberate Adam. Since Adam fell due to the wrongful unity with the archangel, to restore this, the archangel standing in the position of restoration must unite with Adam.

That is, Cain, who stands in the position of the archangel, must unite with Abel, who stands in the position of Adam, to be restored. The failure of Cain and Abel to unite has hindered the establishment of the foundation for unity throughout history and has become the origin of the disruption of the connection of unity. Therefore, Abel must inevitably unite with Cain to prepare the origin of unity to return to God.

So, around whom should the origin of unity be prepared? It must be prepared centered on Adam and Eve, who are united in God's love and God's life. This cannot be achieved by Adam alone. While the fall could happen through both the archangel and Adam, restoration cannot happen through just Adam and the archangel. It must be centered on Abel, who stands in the position of restored Adam, and Cain, who stands in the position of the restored archangel, becoming one to form the foundation of unity.

God desires this, and He has been working for 4,000 years until the time of Jesus. However, we know well that during Jesus' time, although Jesus, standing in the position of Adam, became one with God, he could not unite with John the Baptist, who stood in the position of the archangel, resulting in another failure. Thus, this issue has extended into this era, and we must realize that without addressing this issue through the Unification Church, we cannot form the foundation of unity.

The Path for Unification Church Members
So what path should Unification Church members take today? While it is necessary to fight for the nation and to maintain one's position for the nation, what is even more critical is how I can stand in the position of representing Jesus. Because Jesus Christ, who was sent as God's son throughout history, could not fulfill what he intended to achieve based on the foundation of oneness with God, today, each of us must once again realize this and fulfill it. Without establishing a foundation that connects to what Jesus could not achieve, God's will cannot advance.

You must understand that the foundation of the will ultimately rests with the individual. In this regard, our individual selves are the issue. So, who must I first become one with? I must become one with God's life. How can I become one with God's life? Unless we, as individuals, resolve all the grievances related to the stories and intentions that extended from Jesus' crucifixion, we cannot inherit the foundation of the will that Jesus intended to fulfill.

Because Jesus came to fulfill God's will while receiving God's love, he died without achieving that will, resulting in grievances not only for humanity but also for Jesus himself and God. In other words, because Jesus could not fulfill God's will, grievances have accumulated against God, against Jesus himself, and against the Israelite nation that had been prepared for 4,000 years. As a result, we know that the Israelite nation has not escaped the path of suffering until now. You must understand that without our individual selves resolving these grievances today, we cannot establish the foundation of unity.

So what should you do? The Jesus who came 2,000 years ago and walked the path of labor for 2,000 years has returned to our era to establish 'me' as a representative of Jesus himself. Therefore, we must stand as beings capable of being loved by God or as heirs who can receive God's love. This is an important issue. 

To achieve this, we must subdue the archangel. In other words, you must understand that you are in a position where you cannot avoid subduing Satan. 

What has our Unification Church fought for until now? It has been to subdue the external Cain world before Abel. For that purpose, it has developed from individual struggles to family struggles, tribal struggles, national struggles, and ultimately to struggles on a global scale. This has been our history since the 1960s. 

In the 1960s, we fought to eliminate all external conditions that did not align with Abel's position, but in the 1970s, we must fight to connect and unify all internal and external circumstances that were not achieved centered on Adam. Without this, we cannot establish the foundation of individual Adam victory, family Adam victory, church Adam victory, and national Adam victory.

The activities centered around the 1960s have been a war of attrition to unify the external Cain world. Cain cannot be forced to submit. We must overcome the life force of the world of Satan with God's life force and love Cain more persistently than the world of Satan. Otherwise, we cannot subdue the archangel world, that is, the Cain world. This has been the struggle from the 1960s to the end of the 1970s.

Now, what foundation of unity must we establish? We must prepare the victorious foundation centered on Adam. Until now, we have fought to create an external foundation, but can this external foundation truly serve as a basis to completely subdue the archangel centered on Adam? It has not yet been achieved. The external form and outline have been established, but it has not yet been consolidated into a decisive position. In other words, while there are Abel and Cain, Cain and Abel have not yet become one. That is, the citizens of the Republic of Korea and our church have not yet become one.

While individual Abel and individual Cain have created an environment to personally subdue Cain opposing Abel, overall, this has not been achieved. Additionally, while familial Abel and familial Cain may have fought to allow the representative Cain family to submit before the Abel family, overall, this has not been achieved. Looking at it from the perspective of the church, if the established church represents the Cain position and the Unification Church represents the Abel position, the established church in the position of Cain has not yet entered the stage of submitting to the Unification Church.

Since the 1970s, individual Cain and familial Cain have reached a position where they can be subdued to some extent. When viewed centered on our Unification Church, the teacher has decisively established the foundation of personal victory and family victory. Comparing this to the time of Jesus, we see that Jesus died because he did not have a familial foundation. If he had had a familial foundation, he would not have gone to the cross, but because he did not have that foundation, he went to the cross. Today, our Unification Church is trying to recreate that historical environment to establish a foundation of victory. Because Jesus could not establish a foundation of familial victory centered on the tribal foundation of the Joseph family and the family of Sarah, we have reclaimed this today and prepared the results of victory. This has been the history until the end of the 1970s.

When we started this path with liberation, if a familial foundation centered on the church and the nation had been established, the Korean people and the established church would have aligned with that family based on the will. However, due to the teacher being pursued and chased, the path of individual indemnity, familial indemnity, church indemnity, and national indemnity has remained. Thus, we have walked the path of individual and familial indemnity until now.

The Path of Church and National Indemnity
So, what is the path of indemnity we must now take? We must walk the path of church indemnity and national indemnity. If a familial foundation had been established on the tribal foundation during the time of Jesus, Judaism and the nation of Israel would have been restored at once. However, because Jesus could not fulfill his will and was chased away, history has progressed looking toward personal restoration and familial restoration through a spiritual foundation centered on the Gentiles. However, we have not yet established the forms of nation and ethnicity. We have not yet established the forms of nation and ethnicity in the spiritual realm. Therefore, the gates of heaven in the spiritual world have not yet been opened.

However, today, our Unification Church has established a foundation of Abel's victory that can personally subdue Cain and a foundation of Abel's victory that can subdue Cain on a familial level. Thus, we have reached a position where we can establish a standard of familial victory based on the tribal foundation that was not prepared during the time of Jesus. The issue here is how to absorb the church's foundation through this familial foundation. There must be a period of indemnity for this. This period is from the late 1970s to 1972.

Jesus' desire was to find the tribe and the church. The church was the spiritual center of the Israelite nation, so if the church aligned with Jesus, the nation would automatically follow. The Unification Church now stands in a position to inherit a church foundation that can represent the nation based on the familial victory established on the tribal foundation. Abel and Cain must determine the outcome of their victory and must take a subjective position. The period from 1971 to 1972 is the time to do this, and you must understand that this is the period desired by the will.

If Jesus had united with his family, his tribe, and Judaism, the nation of Israel would have automatically become one. Why? Because the church is the internal center; if the internal center becomes one, the external nation of Israel can automatically move. In this position, if the Unification Church today establishes a relationship with the established church and becomes one, it can establish itself as the Third Israel centered on this land of South Korea. You must understand that we are in a position to determine such a foundation of victory.

Therefore, the question now is how the Unification Church can secure a solid foundation centered on the blessed families. Additionally, even if the teacher's family stands on this foundation, the issue remains whether our Unification Church's blessed families have united centered on the teacher's family. When this is fully united, the tribal foundation will automatically be established.

To subdue the Cain family and the Cain church, the problem now is for the teacher's family and your families to completely align centered on the will. It must be completely aligned. Without this unity, we cannot subdue the Cain church centered on our Unification Church.
is. Therefore, the determination of victory or defeat lies in how completely the teacher's family and your family become one. Since the archangel cannot unite centered on Adam, it is impossible to form the original standard before the fall. Therefore, if the position of the Adam family is that of the teacher's family, then your family must stand in the position of the archangel family and be united with the teacher's family. Without this, it is impossible to form the standard of unity. Centered on God's love, the teacher's family and your family must become one to establish the foundation of unity that can move this nation. You must understand that without this, national liberation is also impossible, and it is not possible to establish the established denominations before the Father's will.

In considering this issue, what should the 1910s be centered around? To unite the established church, which is a Cain-like denomination, we must first organize a family tribal authority that can be formed as an Abel-like denomination in front of the established church. Therefore, you must understand that there is a problem of whether or not to subjugate the established church and establish this nation before the will.

In light of this, to secure a foundation for unity, we must lay the groundwork in blessed families. And how should blessed families establish a foundation for unity? They must go out into the world of Satan and subjugate the families of the Satanic world. Thus, the teacher has been pioneering the path to lead those families centered on the tribal family rights of the Unification Church to unite before the will until today.

How can your family become one centered on the tradition and thought of the teacher's victory? This is the question. You must unite centered on the process that the teacher and the teacher's family have walked. There is no way to unite outside of that process. The process that the teacher's family has walked until now is ultimately the process that your family must also walk. The teacher has walked with the mission of pioneering at the forefront, but you must follow in the position centered on the teacher's family, so you cannot be united without aligning with the teacher's family.

Then, where should we start to achieve this unity? More than uniting within the church, more than uniting within the family, we must unite at the very forefront. We must unite from the front line.

Centered on your family, in front of you are the teacher's family and God, and behind you is Satan. From the perspective of God, the teacher's family is an Abel-like family. Therefore, your family must also stand in the Abel position, yet it remains in the fallen realm of the archangel's world. Even if you stand in the position of an Abel-like family, you are in a position that must subjugate the Cain family.

How should we subjugate the Cain family from here? An Abel-like family cannot subjugate a Cain-like family unless it repeats the path that Abel has walked. What is the formula for walking that path? The formula is the same. Whether it is in the individual, in the family, in the denomination, or in the nation, the scope may widen, but the formula remains the same. The motivation of that formula lies in the relationship between Adam and the archangel centered on God.

The failure to unite the archangel centered on Adam became the motivation for the fall. The archangel played a leading role, and Adam fell because he was drawn by the archangel. Therefore, restoration must be the opposite: Adam must draw the archangel. You must subjugate and draw in families that are in the position of the archangel from the position of the Adam family. This drawing in cannot be done forcibly. It requires the investment of life and love. It requires the consumption of love and life. Centered on the family, not only the parents but also the children must invest life and love; otherwise, restoration is impossible according to the principle. This is why, moving into 1971, we have brought our blessed families to the forefront.

The mission of blessed family women
In bringing families to the forefront, it is necessary to elevate the wife rather than the husband. When looking at the family, the motivation for the fall was not the husband Adam but Eve. Eve broke the path to become one with God by unprincipled unity with the archangel, breaking the path to become God's children and the path to become an eternal ideal couple with Adam. She also completely shattered the kingdom and world of God. Eve was the culprit of this. Because Eve brought about these results, today the women of the Unification Church's blessed families have stepped forward to restore the families of the Satanic world.

This is akin to Eve representing the family before the stage of falling with the archangel. What should the blessed family women, who have taken Eve's place, do? The dispatch of 1,200 blessed families to 120 locations represents the entire number. Although the dispatched locations are on the land of the Republic of Korea, they symbolize not just the limited land of Korea but the whole world. The blessed family women dispatched in this way must embody the position of Eve, who can lead the Cain-like families of the archangel's world, rather than being Eve who fell for the archangel's temptations.

Because Eve fell, God left, and she became an enemy of Adam, and by becoming an enemy of Adam, she became an enemy of the children as well. She became an enemy of her parents, an enemy between couples, and an enemy of her children; this is the retribution of the fall. Therefore, today, countless families on this earth are in a position of enmity between couples and cannot unite in parent-child or sibling relationships. This is the state of fallen families up to now.

Because Eve's fall brought about these results, they must be restored through indemnity. To restore this through indemnity, the women of our blessed families must take on a proactive mission to unite many families that can become enemies of the archangel's world from the position of Eve, representing the Adam family. In other words, they must play a role in subjugating the Cain family, even at the cost of their own lives.

Because Eve fell, God left, Adam left, the connection of true couples left, the connection of true children left, and the connections of true nations and states all left. Therefore, we have sent out 1,200 blessed family women to prepare a fortune that can restore all of this at once.

By doing this, God, who had left, will take an interest again, the husband who had left will regain interest, and the children who had to leave will also take an interest. We will create a time point where the connections of couples, parents, nations, and the world can be gathered into one place. Thus, you must understand that the mobilization of these blessed family women is for this purpose.

Women are in the position of restored Eve, not fallen Eve, so you must unite with these women. When the wife puts in her utmost effort, the husband must also follow suit and match her enthusiasm. The children must also align with this. Blessed families must regard the mobilized women with this mindset. Furthermore, unmarried men and women must serve them with sincerity, treating them as older sisters and older brothers, and become one with them.

This is the reason why blessed family women are at the forefront to restore the Cain family as representatives of the Abel family. At such a time, the teacher's family, your family, and God's family must become one. Who should be elevated to achieve this unity? We must elevate the wife in the position of Eve to unite. Since the fall occurred through Eve, we must establish that point to form a unified foundation and lay the groundwork for families, which is the blessed family wives currently at the forefront.

You must understand that this is not a habitual event like annual outreach. By being mobilized in this way, heaven, families, husbands, and children can become one. Furthermore, when they go out and sacrifice, invest life, and expend love, the families in the Satanic world cannot help but submit.

Because Eve accepted the life of the archangel and the love of the archangel, which became the motivation for the fall, we must share God's love with the archangel's world through Eve. We must give new life to the archangel's world through Eve. By doing this, the connection of life centered on God will be established through heavenly families, and centered on the wives of those connected families, husbands and children will be connected, creating a relationship where Cain-like families can be subdued. In this way, centered on God, the teacher's family and your family will be connected, and when they are connected to Cain-like families, God's life and love will be intertwined, forming the foundation of unity centered on families.

When families become completely one centered on such principles, this will become a new historical event for the Korean people. There has never been anything like this in history. While there have been numerous events throughout history, this kind of event is unprecedented. My grandfather, who had once been prosperous, found himself in dire straits due to the mismanagement of the family wealth by my great-uncle. This led to a loss of reputation and standing within the community, and eventually, my great-uncle left home, unable to face the shame of his actions.

Despite these challenges, my family continued to strive for a better future. The legacy of my ancestors, who had fought for independence and justice, served as a guiding light. They had sacrificed much, and it was our duty to honor their memory by persevering through adversity.

As I reflect on these events, I realize the importance of unity and purpose. Just as my ancestors had worked together for a common cause, we too must come together to fulfill our mission. The struggles we face today are not unlike those of the past, and it is through our collective efforts that we can overcome them.

In this time of challenge, let us remember the sacrifices made by those who came before us. Let us honor their legacy by working diligently towards our goals, ensuring that their dreams for a better future are realized through our actions. Together, we can build a foundation for the generations to come, one that is rooted in love, sacrifice, and unwavering commitment to our shared purpose.

<Prayer> Father, please allow each individual to be able to take responsibility for the unfortunate circumstances of Jesus Christ who came to this earth 2,000 years ago.

The reason God created heaven and earth
God is the Absolute Being. The absolute means that nothing other than one can be tolerated. It is impossible to say, "The thoughts of the Absolute Being are two." If someone thinks that way, they are mistaken. The thoughts of the Absolute Being are clearly one. That thought is eternally absolute from the beginning to the end. No one can demand correction or alteration of it.

Even though the creations of heaven and earth created by such an Absolute Being may not possess absolute value, to have relative value that cannot be separated from the Absolute, one must find the position of "relative absolute" centered on that Absolute. In other words, the fact that we were created by the one and only Absolute Being is evidence that we are beings equipped with the form of "relative absolute." Therefore, the Absolute Being alone cannot have joy. This is because joy cannot be achieved alone.

Why did God create heaven and earth? It is because even the Absolute Being cannot feel joy by Himself, and even if He were to feel joy, He cannot feel the stimulus of joy. In other words, no matter how much the Absolute Being says, "I am the Absolute Being. I am the protagonist of love. I am the protagonist of life," the Absolute Being cannot feel the stimulus of love alone, nor can He feel the stimulus of life that exists within the universe.

For example, no matter how strong a wrestling champion is, if that champion is sitting alone, they cannot know whether they are strong or not. They may seem to have strength, but it might also seem like they do not. When a person is alone without a counterpart, even though they clearly exist, it may seem like they exist or do not exist. This is why the question arises as to why God created heaven and earth.

If someone became the president of the world but all of humanity disappeared, what joy could they feel? They would feel no joy at all. However, if there is even one person left, that one person can bring joy. Who is that one person? It is the one they love. Do you understand? Just having one person to love allows them to rejoice that their long-held dream of becoming the president of the world has finally come true, and they can dance with that person. Why? Because that one person allows for the lineage of the world president to emerge. Thus, they can hope and sing, "Oh my love!" and dance. Right? "Yes."

God is no different. While this may sound exaggerated, God also dislikes being the solitary Absolute Being and needs a counterpart to be with. There must be something to make life enjoyable. There must be something to explore and experience.

"I did not know." If you did not know, then why were you born this way? (Laughter) Think carefully and answer. "Even if there were no sun, the eyes must be born."

Well, the eyes must be born, but they must have been born because someone made them. Someone must have known that when the eyes were born, there was something called the sun. This cannot be denied.

How did the ears come to be so beautifully formed? Before the ears were born, someone must have known that there was air. Look at the nose. Why did the nose come to be this way? You can know whether God exists or not by looking at your eyes, nose, and ears. Those who say God does not exist should take out their eyes, block their ears, and cut off their noses.

If the nose had been placed upside down, what would have happened? (Laughter) It has been designed to prevent such dangers in advance.

Also, knowing that one cannot breathe without air, it has created hairs in the nostrils like a grill. It knows that there is dust in the air. When you look at these things, you might say that God is quite clever; there is a saying that "peace is a bit troublesome," but one could also say that God is quite mischievous. God is indeed quite mischievous.

Look at the nostrils. There are hairs inside the nostrils. However, these hairs do not all gather to one side; they gather in the middle. Right? When dust enters the nostrils, it gets caught in these hairs and mixes with the flowing mucus to harden into boogers. (Laughter) This is not a laughing matter. Do not think too differently about it. I am simply stating what is there.

God has created our bodies as natural bodies that can receive perfect scores. If you look closely at your hair, it resembles a tree. When you rub your hair with your hands, you can tell which side is the root and which side is the opposite. When you rub it, you feel a rough texture when your hand moves from the opposite side toward the root. Because hair is rough, it will surely stick to something if it gets caught.

When you look at the face, what is that dark thing in the middle? It is the eyebrows, right? Why were these placed? If there were no eyebrows, sweat would flow down and make the cute eyes below like a drain. God, knowing that sweat would surely enter the eyes, has placed the eyebrows above the eyes to protect them. And if there were only one eyebrow, that would be problematic. Because there are two, they can flow down without entering the eyes. Additionally, even if there is a traffic jam and sweat flows toward the eyes, God has made the edges of the eyes prominent to prevent it from entering. The eyes are recessed, and the edges are prominent, right? Is that correct? Yes? So, as a work of art, it is perfect. (Laughter)

Now let’s look at the mouth. The tongue can stretch and contract for 70 or 80 years without any problem. It is truly well made. Watching someone eat is mysterious, and listening to them speak is also truly mysterious. Despite the incredibly complex actions that occur, they can eat and speak smoothly in an instant. This is the manifestation of the harmony of heaven and earth. It is truly mysterious. You should be grateful to your tongue. How would you eat and speak without it?

The existence of God
From the moment everything is born, someone must have known what these things should do.

Evolutionists say that an amoeba gradually evolved into a higher animal, a monkey, and that the monkey evolved into a human. But think about it. For a person to exert more power than a human, where must that power come from? The principle of power is such that when it acts, it must be consumed. Here, power must be supplemented for it to continue acting.

When you look at a generator, there is incoming power and outgoing power, and the outgoing power is less than the incoming power. If the incoming and outgoing powers were to become equal, that would be a revolution in the world of power. Supplying gasoline is also to replenish the power that is continually consumed.

When action occurs, consumption takes place, but can an amoeba act and develop? That is a logical contradiction. An amoeba cannot produce higher animals. To do so, there must be a third force that provides support and supply.

From this perspective, it is evident that God knows everything and created accordingly. If one hand were to be straight and the other upside down, moving separately, what would happen? The more you think about it...

The Nature of the Fall and the Method of Salvation
From that perspective, what is the fall? If we explore it through the logic mentioned earlier, we can say that the fall brought about a failure of lineage. Even without the theory of the fall from our principle, we cannot help but arrive at this conclusion. 

So, who is God's enemy? Who is the greatest enemy among God's enemies? Who is the enemy that has prevented humanity's hope from being fulfilled for 6,000 years, during which countless humans and many saints have died? What kind of being is this enemy that has never allowed human hope to be realized throughout this long history of 6,000 years? Who is the greatest enemy among enemies? 

We can forgive an enemy who stole something or cheated us in business. We can forgive an enemy who set fire to our house and destroyed it. However, we cannot forgive an enemy who captured and killed our beloved son or took away our beloved wife. No matter how much we resolve to forgive such an enemy, our teeth grind involuntarily. It is unbearable. An enemy caused by material conditions can be forgotten over time. People with money tend to forget after about 20 years. However, the enemy of love cannot be forgotten, no matter how much time passes. This is because, as time goes by, the pain intensifies. This has been the source of great sorrow in God's providence of salvation until now.

Jesus said, "I tell you, not seven times, but seventy-seven times." (Matthew 18:22) How great is this love! If we were to ask Jesus, "If you forgive someone seventy-seven times, shouldn't Satan be forgiven as well? Is there a note in your doctrine that says to forgive Satan?" would Jesus respond, "Ah, I am the Lord of love, so that is possible"? No, that is not the case.

Christianity states that we humans fell after eating the fruit of the tree of the knowledge of good and evil. Was there poison in that fruit? If so, what kind of absurd God would that be? This is a logical contradiction. When we question them, they cannot respond even in three words and become completely flustered. As a defensive measure to avoid such questions, they say, "Oh! How can humans, who are in a sinful position, dare to question the will of the divine absolute God? That is blasphemy against God."

If a son asks to see what is in his father's beard, a loving father would say, "Oh! Sure," and show it to him. If he wants to see his teeth, the father would say, "Oh! Here you go," and show them. This is the love of a father. Yet, to attach such absurd theories and say, "Don't ask any more questions," is that God's love? If that were the kind of God, I would not believe in Him. If a child sees the hair under his father's armpit and says, "Dad, I want this," the father might grimace at first but then smile again when he sees his child's joy. This is parental love. 

How can it be that humans and God have become such enemies that everything is concealed, and we are told, "This is all you can know"? If that were the case, it would lead to destruction. If God is an absolute counterpart, He would not block anything. He would level the valleys to create a plain, saying, "You and I are interconnected. The outside can also be the inside, and the inside can also be the outside." Only then can we truly become one.

The father must love the son first. The father should not just say to the child, "You, be filial. Be filial." Try doing that for ten years. Where would you find a child who is filial? The father must continuously cover the child with the invisible bundle of love. Only then will the child be filial. That is how it should be. Otherwise, the parent-child relationship will inevitably break.

That is the kingdom of heaven on earth. Until now, you may not have known what the kingdom of heaven on earth is. This is what the kingdom of heaven on earth is.

Today, men must become substitutes for Jesus, and women must become substitutes for Jesus' bride. Men who are older than Jesus must become Jesus' brothers, uncles, fathers, and grandfathers. Likewise, women who are older than Jesus must become Jesus' sisters, aunts, mothers, and grandmothers. Centered around these relatives, if a church is established where heaven and earth can unite and where love can be established eternally, that church will increasingly receive God's grace and develop over time. Do you understand? "Yes." This is the origin of heaven and earth, the origin of eternal life, and the origin that can prosper and be happy forever.

Become a group that resolves Jesus' grievances. This nation and this people are the nation that has appeared as the Israelite people that Jesus wanted to love. Because it is such a nation, even if the established churches oppose our Unification Church, we must know that they are our older brothers whom we must love, and we must devote all our sincerity to loving them. Even if we shed tears of blood, we must love them. When they receive such sincere love, there will be a phenomenon where they will bless us in return.

God first suffers, gives, and loves before taking back. It is not about forcibly taking back from the satanic world, but rather about first loving, suffering, and sacrificing, and then taking back. You must understand that without such a strategy, we cannot leave the origin of world peace.

Today, we are already advancing toward the horizontal world centered on this purpose in the territory of Korea, and we must not lose this joyful and happy time connected to the center that can issue deployment orders. This time, even if it takes countless eons to pass, will not come again. What is happening within the national boundary of restoration during the teacher's time becomes the traditional standard for the new generation and the new heavenly kingdom era. Therefore, to contribute here and leave the conditions of love, you must suffer more than anyone else, sacrifice more than anyone else, and lead the way at the boundary of death to walk the path of heaven. You must become sons and daughters of God.

It is not those who enter the Unification Church and live well who are blessed, but those who enter the Unification Church and suffer, fail, are chased, and experience injustice who are blessed. Therefore, even when difficult circumstances arise before you, you must not run away but confront them. When the nation is in trouble, loyal subjects emerge, and when the family is in trouble, filial sons emerge. The historical tradition until now has been the same in both the heavenly world and the satanic world. Therefore, you are encouraged to voluntarily seek out the more difficult path. Then, this nation will fulfill its priestly responsibilities on behalf of the world, all grievances will be resolved, and the heavenly kingship and the glory of victory will be claimed by our Unification Church. You must know this fact. If the teacher's words are wrong, you can cut off the teacher's head. Because this is the truth, I have faced numerous oppositions from people in the world but have not died or failed.

We Unification Church members must have the conviction that we will not die even if those who oppose us die, and we must resolve to march forward with all our strength and sincerity. Today, I hope that we can become a meaningful group that seeks to resolve the sorrowful grievances left by Jesus on the anniversary of His birth. I ask that all conditions be manifested as results of victory on behalf of Jesus. Do you understand? "Yes." Will you do it or not? "We will." Those who will, please raise your hands.

On this holy day, which is the first of the year, we praise and offer it before You, so please accept it. The Path of Life
