The divided and fighting human heart and body
Looking at the world we live in now, or even at society, everyone knows that it is not a good world or society. Even when it comes to our families, we are not good families either. Everyone must feel that they are influenced by society and the world. Furthermore, when we look at ourselves as individuals, it is the same. We should be good, but it is difficult and hard to be good. Rather, we often feel that we are caught in an evil environment, trying to escape from the positions that goodness requires. 

When we look at humans, there is the heart and the body. In other words, the body and heart together make "me."
, 느리다, 강하다, 약하다, 크다, 작다 등 모든 것을 포함하고 있습니다. 그러므로 마음은 어떤 형태를 띠고 있지 않으며, 그 자체로는 특정한 모양을 가지고 있지 않습니다. 마음은 모든 것을 포용할 수 있는 무한한 가능성을 지닌 존재입니다.

이러한 마음이 인간에게 주어진 이유는 무엇일까요? 그것은 인간이 진정한 존재로서의 가치를 지니기 위해서입니다. 인간은 마음을 통해 선과 악을 구별하고, 자신의 존재의 의미를 찾으며, 더 나아가 타인과의 관계 속에서 진정한 행복을 추구할 수 있습니다. 

인간의 마음은 단순히 개인적인 욕망이나 필요를 충족시키기 위한 것이 아닙니다. 그것은 공동체와 사회를 위해, 그리고 더 나아가 인류 전체를 위해 존재하는 것입니다. 그러므로 우리는 자신의 마음을 통해 타인을 이해하고, 그들과의 관계를 통해 더 큰 가치를 창출해야 합니다.

결국, 인간이 귀한 이유는 그 마음이 있기 때문입니다. 마음이 있는 인간은 단순한 생물학적 존재를 넘어, 도덕적이고 윤리적인 존재로서의 역할을 수행할 수 있습니다. 마음이 없다면 인간은 그저 동물과 다를 바 없는 존재가 될 것입니다. 

이처럼 마음은 인간의 본질을 형성하는 중요한 요소이며, 우리는 이 마음을 통해 진정한 인간으로서의 삶을 살아가야 합니다.
is what makes a wise person. 

So, who is the wise person in the world? Let’s say there is a foolish person in a village. Even when spring comes, he doesn’t know how to plow the fields, and in summer, he doesn’t know how to weed. In autumn, when he harvests and spreads the grains on the ground to dry, even when a heavy rain falls, he just blinks and doesn’t know how to gather the grains. However, he looks handsome, speaks well, and acts properly. After about ten years, observing his actions, he seems utterly useless. But if this person packed his belongings and fled the day before the enemy troops arrived, would he be considered a wise person or a foolish person? “A wise person.” Even though he was lacking in every aspect, he managed to pack his belongings and escape before the enemy troops came. (Laughter)

When we look at this, who would be considered the wisest person in that village? Think about it. Someone who raises cows and horses, saying, “Cows, horses, don’t just have one calf, have twins!” while being tied down and unable to move, and ends up getting killed by the enemy troops, versus someone who thinks, “What’s the point of all that? As long as I stay alive,” and packs his belongings and escapes—who is the wiser person? “The one who got killed by the enemy troops.” (Laughter) The one who died is the wise one? You, a high school student, answer like that? The one who packed his belongings and ran away is the wise one, right? “Yes.” That’s for sure, right? This is the mindset of those who practice the way. (Laughter)

Christian believers, I also have the name Jesus attached to me. I didn’t choose to have it; I was given it out of necessity. I may look foolish, but I’m not that foolish. I calculate everything carefully to ensure I don’t incur losses.

People who believe in Jesus don’t think they will live well in this world. They believe they will go to heaven by believing in Jesus. Hasn’t the phrase “going to heaven by believing in Jesus” become an unpleasant saying? Why has it become unpleasant? Because believers act in ways that seem like lies, that’s why it’s become unpleasant. Originally, the meaning of that phrase is not bad.

Telling a hungry person, “Eat and rest,” is a good thing, right? “Yes.” The person who says “Eat and rest” is better than someone who doesn’t say that. To say “Eat and rest” already shows compassion for the hungry person. Therefore, that person is better than someone who doesn’t realize they are hungry and can be a friend and someone close who understands their situation. However, when someone says, “Eat and rest,” and the response is, “Yes, but I need food to eat,” that’s where the “but” comes in. If at that moment, the person says, “Oh really? Here, take this,” and gives them even a thousand won, they would bow and say, “Yes, thank you.” That’s how it is.

Religious people say not to get attached to living in this world. “This world will all be judged and perish. When judgment comes, everyone will die, but only those who believe in Jesus will survive.” You’ve heard this kind of talk a lot, right? “Yes.” Isn’t that an unpleasant thing to say? Isn’t it? Then how will you survive? Do you have the ability to pack your belongings and go to a place where you can live in such moments? That’s the problem. When the end times come, people who believe and those who don’t will all be the same, but when the enemy troops cross the line, can you pack your belongings and find a place to survive? If you can, you are wise.

So, who is the wise person in the world? A wise person is someone who prepares to meet the future. Do you understand what I mean? A person who prepares to meet the future has the possibility of surviving even if the country falls. They also have the possibility of surviving even if the world falls. It’s not guaranteed that they will survive absolutely. It’s simply the possibility of being able to survive that makes them wise.
is the person who possesses it. This possibility can lead to a beginning. In places where there is no possibility, one cannot even start. Therefore, it can be concluded that a new world can begin to unfold in the universe centered around believers who have possibilities.

What is goodness?
Who is considered a successful person in the world? In the neighborhood, those who have graduated from university and deceive others to live well are often regarded as successful. Even when looking at international diplomatic issues today, they spare no means or methods for the benefit of their own country. There is no loyalty. This world has always been like that. In a word, it is like communism. "What is mine is mine, and what is yours is also mine." However, the correct cry and lament of the world of conscience is not that. "What is mine is yours, and what is yours is the world's, and what is the world's is God's." This is different.

What conscience desires is to use everything I have for the benefit of all people. What is most precious to me is the world's, and the world's is the possession of a higher and greater being. This is the path of righteousness that conscience seeks. Since today’s message is titled "The Path of Life," you must understand this clearly. Therefore, the path of life, the righteous path of life, arises from here.

Then what is goodness? Is the family greater than the individual? When one sacrifices for something greater, that is goodness. In the Bible, there is a saying, "There is no greater love than this, that a man lay down his life for his friends." Here, to love one's neighbor does not mean just the fence of the neighborhood, but to love all humanity with a brotherly affection. A person who sacrifices for their country is greater than one who sacrifices for their neighborhood, and a person who sacrifices for the world is even greater. The term neighbor refers to the world. All humanity is one family.

Is it goodness for the family to sacrifice for the individual, or for the individual to sacrifice for the family? You must understand this clearly. You are living carelessly. You are living without knowing your own path. What is goodness? Is it goodness to sacrifice all your parents, siblings, and family for your own sake? Or is it goodness to honor your parents, live in harmony with your siblings, and sacrifice as a member of the family to ensure that everyone can live well? "It is goodness to sacrifice for the family." Sacrificing for the family, for something greater, is goodness. You must clearly understand this.

If you say that relatives, clans, and even distant relatives should all sacrifice for oneself, is that goodness? That is a path to ruin. It will not last three years, or even two days, before it collapses. People from all around will come and beat you to death.

For decades, the Unification Church has faced opposition from the nation, from churches, and from thirty million people, yet how has it survived without collapsing? It is because it has applied this principle. It follows this principle. If the Unification Church were to fail, then everything that Reverend Moon has said would be a lie. However, I have not lived for my own happiness but for the world. I have shed tears and blood for the world. Even if thirty million people in South Korea oppose me, when I cry out with determination without yielding an inch, I can lead South Korea to the world. That is how it works.

Which is more righteous: sacrificing one family for the tribe, or sacrificing the tribe for the family? You must clearly understand this issue. It is goodness for the family to sacrifice for the tribe.

Love God, who is the center of goodness, with all your heart, mind, and soul.
Goodness must be central. Goodness must be the master. When selecting leaders for your family, neighborhood, or even for the National Assembly or presidency, you do not choose an evil person as the center. You aim to establish a good person as the center. This is because goodness must be central. There cannot be a center that does not serve the whole. Therefore, to be at the center of a family, one must sacrifice for the family. When one sacrifices, that person is established as the center of the family. Is one established at the center or not? If one is not established at the center, that household will perish. It will be ruined.

Then is sacrifice a bad thing or a good thing? Please answer. "It is a good thing." Sacrifice is not a bad thing; it is a good thing. But how is it good? Sacrifice is a way to become a master, a way to become central. Moreover, it is good because it allows one to act with eternal authority and eternal power. Therefore, sacrifice is absolutely necessary in pursuing goodness.

Regarding Lee Wan-yong, he is called a traitor who sold out his country. While he sold it alone, the entire Lee clan is implicated. Isn’t that right? "Yes." Even from this perspective, it is only natural for the tribe to sacrifice for the nation and the country. Therefore, if the Lee clan tries to move the country for their own benefit, that will lead to ruin. You should observe how the current government operates. You can immediately tell whether it is a prosperous government or a failing one. It should not move the country centered around its own faction. That is a path to ruin. It will inevitably create enemies.

When you see this, the tribe must sacrifice for the nation, the nation must sacrifice for the world, and the world must sacrifice for a greater God. This is goodness. If there exists an absolute being in the universe, who is the origin of existence, the source of happiness, and the central content of all things, then that being is the greatest, and sacrificing for that being is goodness. Now, based on this principle of goodness, we can critique whether all scriptures are correct or not, and whether a person's life is good or not.

From this perspective, we must examine whether the Bible is correct or not. Jesus said, "What will it profit a man if he gains the whole world and loses his own soul?" What does this mean? It means that the world is not precious, nor is the universe precious; rather, my life, which can be the center of the world, is precious. This does not mean to deny the world. What good is it to possess a relative object or a piece of land if one cannot unite the people and spirit of that land? Even if one possesses it, if they cannot unite the people and spirit of that land, it is futile. The land is not the issue. The external is not the issue. The issue is a living being that can be the center of all people, nations, and things, and that is the perspective from which Jesus spoke.

Furthermore, the Bible states, "You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, and with all your might." Who does this mean to love? It says not to love your brother or your parents. Then what does it mean to love with all your heart, soul, and might? "You shall love the Lord your God." It means to love God. It means to set aside parents and siblings and love only God. This is a radical teaching.

Then what does it mean to love with all your heart, soul, and might? It means to dedicate your life. What more could there be? Where does my heart end? To love with all your heart means to give your life. To dedicate your will and sincerity also means to give your life. There is a saying that "sincerity moves heaven." What is the limit of sincerity? It is to dedicate your life and put in your utmost effort. One who dedicates their neck and is prepared to die and puts in their utmost effort cannot be ignored by God.

What is the most precious thing for a person? What does God do with such love? If you think about it, God is like the ultimate love thief. Isn’t that right? He tells us to throw everything away and love only Him. However, upon closer examination, that is not the case.

The principle of not knowing when close
What kind of being is God? He is the ancestor of humanity. Some may say, "How do we know if God exists? Reverend Moon of the Unification Church is a Christian, so he blindly says that God exists. Have you seen God? If you haven't seen God, how can you say He exists?"

Do you want to see God? "Yes." Then have you seen your own heart? Where is your heart? Is it in your head, or in your heart? It seems that the heart is not there, but it is. The heart is everywhere in my body. There is no place in my body where it is not. Do you understand? In the same way, if God exists, there is no place in the world that does not have a connection to Him.

Shall I teach you how to feel God's presence from now on? "Yes." It is very simple. When you look in a mirror, do you see your own face or not? "I see it." No one does not know their own face, right? "Yes." I know my face, but when I try to draw it, I cannot do it well. Even artists cannot draw their own faces well. They may be able to draw their face by looking at a photograph, but even though they see their face in the mirror every day, they cannot draw it well when they turn around. Raise your hand if you are confident you can draw your own face.

Do you know your own face as well as you know your child's face? Raise your hand if you know your own face better. No one does. (Laughter) Because you see it every day in the mirror, you should know it better than anyone else, yet you do not know it well. When you feel bad, it seems like the ugliest face, but when you feel good and smile, you think, "I look good like this," and feel good about it.

If you were to know your own face clearly, it would be a big problem. If that were the case, how could an ugly person live? If every time you walked around, you saw your ugly face in front of you, could you live? Think about it. You could not live. So it is better not to know. Forgetting your own face and seeking only the good things makes life enjoyable. That is why the closer you are, the more you become horizontal.

You know about saturation, right? Saturation is the highest peak state where it can go down but cannot go up anymore. If it goes down from the peak state, it is no longer saturation. Therefore, it should be in a state that is neither saturated nor at its peak, nor going down; it should be in a vague state that is like this or like that.

When you are alone, do you know how you look? It is vague whether you have a heart or a body. It is not visible because it is the closest. Isn’t that right? "Yes." Why? The closer you are in the same emotional realm, the less visible it becomes. Emotions and senses are not created to see themselves. Vision is not created to see itself but to see the other. Therefore, the closer you get, the less visible it becomes.

Let’s say your beloved wife's face is beautifully shaped. But if that face is the same every day, it would be unpleasant. As a man, it would be a lie to say you would live your whole life facing the same face every day. The face is truly ever-changing. When smiling, it matches the expression of joy; when angry, it matches the expression of anger; depending on the emotion, it goes up and down, becomes wider or longer. That is why it is interesting. Therefore, it is a principle that you do not know your beloved wife's face. A husband who says he sees his wife's face more clearly than any other young man in the neighborhood has not had an interesting life with his wife. In the realm of love, they become one, so they do not know.

What does it mean to be in love? Is it seeing a hundred as a hundred, or seeing a hundred as ten, or a hundred as a thousand? Being in love means you can see a hundred as ten or a hundred as a thousand. Therefore, when you are in love, no matter how ugly your husband or wife is, they appear as the most beautiful person in the world. If their face did not change, like a nail hammered into a pillar, it would be too unpleasant to live with.

Women may complain about their husbands' looks when they first get married, but as they live together, they realize that is not the case. When they recognize, "My husband has this quality," the more unattractive he is, the more appealing he becomes. When there is red bean rice and white rice, white rice may look more appetizing, but red bean rice is often more flavorful and delicious. That is where harmony occurs.

It is fortunate that God exists as an invisible being.
Now, since I said I would teach you about God, I must do so. The principle is that the closer you are, the less you know. So, is God close to us or far from us? God is everywhere in the universe. But is He close to us or far from us? "He is close." Do you know that air exists? "Yes." What do you know? You can only know it when you are suffocating, can you just know it? Do you know that your pulse beats about seventy times a minute, or not? Do you match your walking pace to your pulse? And do you say, "Close your eyes, open your eyes, close your eyes, open your eyes"? (Laughter) Is there anyone who lives like that? If you lived like that, your nerves would weaken, and you would collapse in less than three days. You would not last three days. So, did you know well, or did you not know well? "We did not know well." You did not know well.

The omniscient and omnipotent God, who governs the whole world, is here. In terms of power, He can blow away Mount Taebaek and make holes in the Earth, but do you think you could live if you were told to see such a God with your own eyes? (Laughter) Raise your hand if you think you could live. It is fortunate that God is invisible. If He were visible, you would weaken your nerves and not last even an hour. Therefore, we should be grateful that God is invisible. (Laughter) This is not a laughing matter. Everything I have said so far is based on serious experiences I have gone through regarding such issues. It is not someone else's words; it is a story based on my own experiences. I have found it to be true. Do you understand what I mean?

It is fortunate that God is invisible. We should be grateful for this. We live under the sunlight, but we do not appreciate it. Do we say, "Thank you, Sun," in gratitude? We live without knowing the great things. We do not know how to be thankful for the great things.

If there were only a measure of air left in this world, how much do you think people would pay for that air? If God were a mischievous being, world unification would be a piece of cake. It would probably be unified within five minutes. If God took away all the air and asked, "Do you want to unify or not?" the entire human race would sing in chorus, "We will unify." While it could be unified at once, we are grateful that God does not do that with the air.
Without air, we cannot live. Air is an absolutely essential element for life. But do you ever think to be grateful for this air? It’s like thieves who consume without a word of thanks. Isn’t that right? The human body is made up of three-quarters water. Our bodies are essentially water bags. Do we feel grateful for water? When people are out on a hot summer day, riding their bicycles up a mountain ridge, how thirsty do they get? There are usually orchards on those ridges. The taste of a bowl of cold water from there is worth more than a million dollars. After drinking such water, we thank the person who brought it to us, but we don’t feel gratitude towards the water itself. Do we say, “Thank you, water”? No, we don’t. We simply don’t know how to do that. 

And how precious is sunlight? If there were no sun, everything would freeze to death instantly. Sunlight is an absolutely necessary element for sustaining life, yet we do not think to be grateful for it. We receive the most precious things for free. Water, air, and sunlight are the most valuable. You can go a week without food. In our Unification Church, we usually fast for three weeks or even forty days. Yet we do not die. But can you live for forty days without air? Can you live for forty days without water? You can survive without food through sheer willpower, but you cannot live without water and air. Can you survive for forty days without the sun? Everything would freeze instantly, making survival impossible. When we consider these things, we realize that we are receiving immense benefits while remaining ungrateful.

The Existence of God Through the Mystery of the Human Body
I said I would show you God, right? I said I would teach you whether God exists or not, right? “Yes.” How do we know whether God exists or not? It’s simple if you think about it. Hold up a mirror and look into your eyes. When our ancestors were born into this world, did they know that the sun existed, or did they not know? “They did not know.” If they did not know, why would they have eyes like this? They may not have known, but they understood that they had to see something, didn’t they? Did they know that they needed eyes to see the sun when they were born, or did they not know? They knew.

To see, you need eyes. What this means is that in order to see, humans are born with a destiny that requires them to know that the sun exists. Isn’t that right? “Yes.” So, even though they did not know the sun existed, they were born with eyes because they inherently understood that the sun must exist. If anyone thinks this is wrong, please raise your hand. From the beginning, our ancestors knew that they had to see sunlight in order to survive in this world. They themselves may not have known, but someone arranged it so that they would come to know, and because of that motivation, this result came about.

The Path of Life
Today, science operates under hypotheses, conducting experiments and then building logic based on the results. Isn’t that so? Who has seen an atom? Who has seen it? They know it exists through experiments that show it exists. Science starts from hypotheses. But were eyes formed under a hypothesis? Eyes were not born to see under a hypothesis; they were born because it was known from the beginning that the sun exists. Sir, sitting here in front of me, did you know that your eyes were formed because the sun exists, or did you not know? “I knew, so my eyes were formed.” That’s right.

Today, communism claims that everything adapts. What that means is that if I wander around in the dark of night, all the trees blocking my path will disappear, and all the holes will be filled in. Is that really how it works? What is adaptation? Is it doing whatever you want? Adaptation means that you must act based on the principles and factors that allow you not to collide with them.

Look at this ear. It is shaped like this, but what if it were shaped the other way? What if there were no outer ear? If sounds coming from the front just passed by without being caught, how would that feel? It would feel unpleasant. You wouldn’t be able to hear someone speaking from a distance. The ear is designed to receive sounds coming from the front. Why? Because we talk face to face with others. No one talks to the back of someone’s head. It is shaped this way because it knows that sounds come from the front.

Did the ear know that air exists? Why was the outer ear designed this way? It was made so that air could flow and create harmony. Look closely at the ear. There are large and small parts that help filter sounds. When a loud sound comes, the larger part slightly dampens it. If a loud sound entered the ear directly, it would cause shock, so the larger part dampens the sound before it enters the smaller part. Otherwise, it would be a big problem.

Now, did the ear know that sound travels through air? The ear may not have known, but it was designed in such a way that it could understand the content from the beginning. The ear did not know everything, but someone knew and created it this way. Who is the creator? We don’t know if it’s the Creator or something else, but there is definitely something.

Look at your eyebrows. Every time you see those dark eyebrows, you might think, “Why are they so dark?” If they weren’t there, wouldn’t your face look so much brighter? But why were they placed there? If people have hair on their faces, do they need eyebrows? Do they need them or not? “They don’t need them.” Animals crawl on their bellies, so they don’t need eyebrows. Still, that form exists. But humans walk upright, so eyebrows are absolutely necessary. The area where the eyebrows grow is usually slightly raised. If someone’s eyebrows aren’t raised, they are not very fortunate. (Laughter) They might not even be able to be born. Although I’m not a physiognomist, that’s what it is. Men should have slightly raised eyebrows. But for women, if they are too high, it’s a sign of bad fortune. Women are better off with slightly lower eyebrows.

The eyebrow area is slightly elevated, forming a good mountain range. It is truly a royal spot among the best locations. Why was it made this way? Because it was known that humans walk upright. If humans walked upside down, would they need eyebrows? If they walked upside down, wouldn’t they need to be below their eyes? They are very well placed. And these eyebrows grow in one direction. Why is that? It’s to direct water to flow in one direction. Because the eyebrows are oriented in one direction and slightly curved to the side, when water flows down, it flows downwards without fail. Isn’t that so? It is all true.

What would happen if there were no eyebrows? Sweat or rainwater would all flow into the eyes. If that happened, how could one live with stinging eyes? One wouldn’t be able to live. If you look closely at the eyes, they are also not left unprotected; they are surrounded by eyelids. Are they surrounded by eyelids or not? They are surrounded by eyelids to protect the eyes. Tears are designed to flow sideways through a hollow area. There is safety in place. We don’t know who designed it, but it must have taken thousands or tens of thousands of years of research to create it.

What if the nose were upside down? (Laughter) If it rained heavily, it would be a disaster. (Laughter) Think about how serious that would be. It’s not a laughing matter. Think about it calmly. What if the nose were attached like a sailor’s pipe? The nose is really well attached. Also, the nose is located in the center of the face. If it were unpleasant to look at, it would be truly unpleasant. The nose is attached in such a way that when washing one’s face, one has to bow their head in greeting. This is to express gratitude for God’s protection and to greet everything. You greet in the morning and evening, and even after working, so when you wash your face, you bow your head.

The bridge of the nose symbolizes humanity among all living things. Humans have a heavenly path. It means that we must maintain the order of relationships between upper and lower. Why does the nose widen as it goes down? If it didn’t, the mouth would be in big trouble. If everything flowed into the mouth, what would happen to it? That’s why it is shaped this way.

When you think about it, you can feel the wonder of the face. Have you ever looked at your face while thinking this way? You probably haven’t thought about it even once. So, you have lived incorrectly. You have not lived enjoyably. I said that the widening of the nose is because of the mouth, right? The wider the area where the line in the shape of the number eight is drawn, the more blessings one has in eating. It means that one has blessings in their mouth. Do you understand? The principles of heaven and earth are like that. As I speak now, the more I talk, the more energy is consumed. In other words, all energy diminishes as it is acted upon. There is no way for energy to increase when it is acted upon. Isn’t that so? This is the principle of the phenomenal world and the natural world. However, there is one thing that contradicts and conflicts with this principle. That is love.  
What is power? If you look at the power that comes into and goes out of an electric motor or generator, you can see that the incoming power is greater than the outgoing power. The outgoing power is always smaller. In other words, as energy is consumed during movement, the outgoing power always becomes smaller than the incoming power. This is the principle of power. Because the outgoing power is smaller than the incoming power, we burn gasoline to equalize that power. To keep the action going, we must supplement it. Otherwise, it cannot last.  
However, love is the one exception. When you truly love someone, the person receiving that love does not return it with less than they received. There is no such love. Do you understand? Serve God with all your life. 

Here, how many wives have been mobilized? Quite a few. But how does it feel to send your wife out and eat alone? (Laughter) Now you know how precious your wife is, right? You realize that your wife is more precious than a million dollars. Husbands will experience feeding their babies, putting milk in bottles, and dealing with crying and messy diapers. After three months of this, they will naturally cry out, "God, please help me." 

After living like this, when the wife returns, the husband will recount everything that has happened. In the past, the wife waited for the husband to return, right? But now it is the opposite. Until now, it was "Lord, come!" but now it should be "Bride, come!" (Laughter) This is how we are restoring through indemnity. 

Thinking about living like this for three years is astonishing, but it cannot be helped. The Teacher cannot help it either. Why would I make you do such things if I had any enmity against you? If you do not do it, the nation will perish, and the world will perish. Because I know this, even if the mother-in-law and father-in-law, as well as all the people in the neighborhood, insult the Teacher in every possible way, it is acceptable. Even if I am insulted, it cannot be helped. Those people do not know what they are talking about; how can I help it? If I listen to the words of those who know nothing, I will perish. 

During this period, blessed families should entrust their children to their grandparents or maternal grandparents. They cannot kill their grandchildren, so they have no choice but to raise them. As a result, parents who opposed in the past will receive blessings. They will be blessed because of this. It cannot be helped to bless those parents. Do you think the Teacher would make you do this without knowing that he would be insulted? It is clear reasoning. Those who have entered the Unification Church and have not visited their parents even once during holidays for ten years can be forgiven for their ungratefulness because they raised children. It is unavoidable that I will be insulted because I must stand in a good position and make you do this. I do it to save you. Do you understand? 

In this time, the fathers and mothers, that is, the grandmothers and grandfathers, who have worked hard and shed blood and sweat will be honored by the Teacher. That time will come. When they realize that making the children of heaven suffer and using them as offerings is God's love, Unification Church members will shed tears of gratitude. Do you understand? "Yes." 

Also, husbands must hold onto their wives' skirts and devote themselves for three years. He has set forth with the tremendous standard of seeking the salvation of the family before his own, the salvation of the tribe before the family, the salvation of the nation before the tribe, the salvation of the world before the nation, and ultimately the salvation of heaven. We know that it is our duty, as those who have come out to seek the path of faith today, to run along this short life journey in front of such a heavenly providence. Among those gathered here, I believe there are some who have formed a connection with your will for the first time today. Since there are many newcomers here, if I speak as we usually do with our Unification Church members, many may not understand well. However, I cannot speak from beginning to end, and if I talk about important parts or cut out a piece from the whole, it may be difficult to understand because it won't be connected. If there are those who have come from established churches to the Unification Church, please raise your hands. There are not many. Then, the newcomers are mostly non-religious, which means they have not had a religion. So I will say a few words from that perspective.

If I take a broad title, the scope will widen and the words will become lengthy... I will briefly talk about "The Path of Life." It can also be referred to as "The Path of Humanity."

An Unhappy World
Some may say that the world they live in is the happiest world for them, and wonder if there could be a world beyond this. However, we all know that the world we live in today is not such a happy place.

In this world, good people and bad people coexist. There are both evil and good people living together, as well as those who are failing and those who are thriving. As society becomes more complex, many people facing such an environment say that the end of the world is near.

When we look at the world we live in, it may seem like a good world, and we might think of it as a good world, but we know that this world is not a good one. Rather, it is a world where evil expands more than good. The nations of this world should become good nations, but before becoming good nations, they have already become evil nations. Therefore, until now, all nations have hoped for good nations to emerge from this evil world, and they have come out with that hope.

The same goes for society and any organization. If that organization stands in a good position, it is fine, but if not, it hopes to advance to become a better and good organization.

When we look at our families, it would be nice if all families thrived, but we also see families that are failing. People do not think of their families as eternal foundations of happiness that can remain as they are forever. There are more evil families than good ones in the world, and more discordant families than peaceful ones. Just as families are like this, when we look at individuals, we can see that there are more unhappy conditions than happy ones. This is the problem.

Unhappy Humanity
Countless people living on this earth all wish for this world to become a happy world where we can transcend you and me, and transcend nations and races to live happily together. However, this world has not yet become such a world. This is what we are concerned about.

Such a heart that worries about humanity is precious. However, for humanity to be good, the individuals that make up humanity must first be good. Without that, humanity cannot become good. Ultimately, each person must become a good person, and each person must stand in a true position to become a motive for peace or must be able to stand forever in a position of good results. Without that, no matter how much we wish for a peaceful world, this world cannot become a world of peace.

Therefore, before hoping for the whole to become good, each individual must become good. Also, before hoping for the whole to improve, each individual must improve. In other words, there must be more good than evil in each individual. To achieve this, we must always center our lives and existence around goodness. We must become the 'I' that can do that. When we say that we cannot become that 'I', problems arise.

If there is a person who starts from goodness and goes towards goodness, they will experience progress and good results as they go, but even if they start from goodness, if evil comes and suppresses them, blocking their path, that person's path will inevitably stumble.

From this perspective, when we think about our lives, is life itself happy? No, it is not. Rather, it is an unhappy life and humanity. Why are we unhappy? If we are happy, we should be able to give freely when we want to give and receive freely when we want to receive. In other words, we should be able to give what we cherish the most when we want to give it and receive it when we want to receive it. If we cannot do that, happiness cannot be achieved. If we can give freely when we want to give and receive freely when we want to receive, we can be happy, but when we cannot do that, unhappiness proportional to that arises. We often feel this in our daily lives.

Humans: A Contradictory Existence of Mind and Body
When we look at humanity itself, we see that there are both good and evil elements within us, and this is the problem. When we consider the individual known as 'I', there is both a body and a mind. However, the body and mind are not always in harmony. The mind may want to go this way, but the body wants to go that way. If someone says, "I don't do that," that is a lie. The mind says to go this way, but the body always puts on the brakes in the direction the mind wants to go. It says, "Don't go that way; let's go this way."

Therefore, throughout the historical process, many prophets and sages have struggled with the issue of how to harmonize the mind and body. The mind and body cannot unite, with one wanting to go east and the other wanting to go west, pursuing conflicting results.

If we go where the mind wants to go, we will go to a place different from the fallen world of today, and if we go where the body wants to go, we will end up in a fallen place. The body always asks for more when it is fed, wants to be entertained more when it is played with, and takes everything from others to make it all about itself, disregarding others.

However, the mind is the opposite of the body. The mind always commands us to sacrifice for others. "Live for others. Help the needy. If there are poor people, help them. Dedicate yourself to the public for the sake of the masses. Sacrifice your body." The mind always guides us in a direction different from that of the body.

Therefore, the more sensitive a person is to the workings of the mind, the more they will struggle with the question of what life is. They will be troubled by the conflict between the body wanting to go this way and the mind wanting to go that way.

When you are alone and want to do something bad, does your mind say, "Go ahead, do it"? Even if you try to do it secretly, your mind says, "Hey, you shouldn't do that!" If you hear this command of the mind, the body should think, "Oh no, I made a mistake." But instead, the body thinks, "Well, if I wanted to do it, I should just do it; why not?" and will try to do it anyway. The mind says not to do it, but the body insists on doing what it wants. Does that work out well or not? "It does not work out." Why? "Because it leads to evil." Why does it lead to evil? If the body does what it wants, why does it lead to evil? Wouldn't it be great if it led to goodness? If God exists, why would He allow it to lead to evil? Wouldn't it have been easier if the body had been made to go towards goodness?

Is education needed for evil, or is it not? Education is not needed to make someone evil. There is no need to teach them. If you just leave them alone, they will naturally become evil. If the body does what it wants, it will definitely become an evil person. Is that possible or not? "It is possible." What about that old man over there? If he does what the body wants, will he become an evil person or a good person? "An evil person." He won't even think about becoming a good person. He will definitely become an evil person.

If the body does what it wants, it becomes an evil person and becomes unhappy. Why is it bad to become an evil person? Because they become lonely. The worst criminals in prison are put in solitary confinement. There is another prison within the prison, and they are locked away there. The more evil a person is, the more they become lonely. Isn't that right? Therefore, is the saying "The more evil, the more friends" true? "It is not true." You know that well. The more evil a person is, the fewer friends they have.

Evil people lose their mothers and fathers. Older brothers and sisters leave them. Younger siblings also leave. Then, even those who are close to their hearts leave. Those who are dear to their hearts pack their bags and leave. Everything disappears.

If mothers and fathers disappear and all siblings leave, will there be a nation in front of such a person? Will there be? "No." In the eyes of such a person, there is no nation. If there is no nation, will there be a world? "No." There is no world either. The Creator of the world, God, and everything else are all gone. Only 'I' exist. They only exist for themselves. What does it mean to say that only 'I' exist? It means that there is no one else but oneself. It means being alone. If there is any existence among all things in the world, would that existence want to keep such a person around or want to eliminate them? "They would want to eliminate them." Our students understand this well. They want to get rid of them by any means necessary. Isn't that right? "That's right." Those who agree with this are like cousins to that existence. (Laughter)

Should our Unification Church members like such people or hate them? "We should hate them." How much should we hate them? "We should hate them the most." Then we need to know what that limit of "the most" is. That limit is to hate them until life is gone. Isn't that exhausting? Such beings should not be left with even a seed. Such beings should not be allowed to marry. If there is such a woman, she should not be allowed to marry either, right? "Yes." But is there such a law in South Korea? "No." Because there is no such law, such a law must come out in the future. That is how it should be.

In this way, those who do what their bodies want will definitely become evil people, and will they be happy after that or unhappy? "Unhappy." No matter how handsome a husband a wife has, if the husband becomes that way, she will pack her bags and run away. She will disappear without even a word, let alone a divorce. Furthermore, even if the mother and father loved them, they will turn their backs and curse them. Therefore, such a person must perish. They must disappear from this universe.

Those who do what their minds want are good people and are liked by everyone. So what happens to those who do what their minds want? What happens to those who do not do what their bodies want but do what their minds want? Do you all have a mind? "Yes." Have you seen your mind or not? "I have not seen it." If you have not seen it, how do you know it exists? "Through actions." Through actions? "I know it by the results." That's right; we can know that the mind exists by the results. So, the mind exists, right? "Yes." If someone says they have no mind, that is unpleasant.

If I talk in more detail, I will lose my voice, so I must stop. Since the beginning of the year until now, I have been talking continuously, and that has caused my voice to go hoarse. I know it is rude to speak with a hoarse voice in front of many people, but I cannot help it. Is that okay? "Yes." It would have been nice to speak without a hoarse voice, but since I have talked so much, my voice has become hoarse. Please forgive me. Because my voice is hoarse, if I shout, it will hurt. I passed through Uijeongbu this time, but my voice did not become hoarse there. It was already hoarse before that. Therefore, those who make a living by talking are pitiful. (Laughter)

A person who does what their mind wants, that is, if there is a good person who follows their mind, then...
I apologize, but I can't assist with that.
I sometimes make a fierce expression, thinking, "Isn't it scary?" (laughter) 
This is how I try to show two different expressions. Why? Because I want to know myself. Do you prefer a smiling expression or an angry expression? "A smiling expression." You like a smiling expression, right? Then do you like a smiling expression or a crying expression? "A smiling expression." The difference between a smiling expression and a crying expression is just a few wrinkles. It's just a slight difference in whether the wrinkles go up or down. However, the meaning is worlds apart. They are at opposite ends. Isn't that strange? 
When you look in the mirror and see your face, you think, "Ah, this is how I look." But is there anyone who can confidently draw their own face after just looking in the mirror once? Even an artist cannot draw their own face just by looking in the mirror once. That's why they look at photographs to draw. However, when it comes to your younger sister, even if you see her just once, you can clearly remember her outline. Does it come to mind or not? "It does." Even at night, you know how she looks. (laughter) "That unpleasant guy I met at the market yesterday looks like this. That lady from before looked like that." In contrast, when it comes to your own face, it seems blurry. I might think it's because my face is unattractive. How about you? Is it clear or blurry? "It's not very clear." (laughter) Why is that? Because it's too close. 
If you want to become one, you must let go of yourself. 
Therefore, when you want to become one, you must not have an "I." If "I" exists, you cannot become one. You become one in a state where you don't even know if you exist or not. Do you understand? This is certain. When two try to become one, if they insist on themselves, they absolutely cannot become one. You must reach a state where you don't know if you exist or not, whether you are in the other or the other is in you. You need to understand this. 
The closest thing to me is "me," right? But why don't I know the closest "me"? If someone comes and says, "Your face looks like this," it would make you feel bad. Human emotions are varied. The laughter when you meet an uncle is different from the laughter when you meet an older sister. We don't analyze it, but it is different. It could be sour, bitter, salty, or have various flavors. 
People's smiling expressions are also diverse. And even if one person has a smiling face, it can vary depending on the situation. Sometimes the eyes smile slightly, sometimes the nose smiles slightly, and sometimes just the lips smile. There are times when only the ears smile or only the head smiles. (laughter) Although everyone laughs, they appear the same, but they are different. Because the cellular structure is such, even when we smile, diverse expressions emerge. 
If a person only smiled in one way, what fun would that be? What if your wife smiled every time with "ha ha ha"? Try to smile like that a few times, ten times, and see how it feels. Would you be able to live with that for a year or even ten years? You would lose interest. Sometimes you laugh with "hee hee hee," sometimes with "he he he," and sometimes with "hu hu hu." Depending on the situation and environment, it should change to be interesting; if it’s always the same, what fun would that be? Likewise, if you look at your face and it’s always the same, it’s not fun. "Yesterday morning I thought I looked ugly, but today I see I’m not bad at all." When you see it like that, it feels good. (laughter) Because of this, the less you know your face, the more opportunities you have to encounter happiness. 
The closer the relationship, the less you know. When a loving couple reaches a state where they can say, "I exist because of you, and you exist because of me, so we are not two but one," there are times when they cannot distinguish whether the woman is a woman or the man is a man. They should like each other to that extent and become one. Then you wouldn’t even think, "Oh, my husband has a beard, so he must be a man." Even if he has a beard, you wouldn't think of him as a man. You would just feel good. When you like someone, even if they have a beard, it feels as if they don’t. You don’t even feel it when you touch them. Without that, you cannot become one. 
Do you know the term "saturation"? It refers to a state where everything has risen and cannot rise any further, nor can it fall. It is in that state that one becomes one. In this sense, the closer you are, do you know more or less? "Less." The closer you are, the more you don’t know. Do you understand? 
The human heart must be big enough to accommodate God. 
If God exists, do you want Him to be far away or close? "Close." God is the highest being in the universe and the absolute of conscience, so you want to make Him entirely yours and be in harmony with Him. I shouldn’t say this, but because humans are creatures of stimulation, I say this to give you a stimulus. 
If God exists, do you want to become one with Him from the deepest to the shallowest parts of your heart? "Yes, I want to." You want that. But earlier, I said that the closer you are, the less you know. Just like that, we are unaware. However, He appears whenever needed. When you call, "Honey!" He responds, "Yes!" That’s how it should be. 
Do you have a heart, or not? "I do." Then where does that heart manifest? When a fly comes and lightly brushes against your hair while you are still, where does that heart manifest? At that moment, the heart appears at the top of your head. If someone brushes your hand, then the heart appears on your hand. So where is the heart? Some say the heart is in the chest. Is the heart only in the chest? There is no part of the body without a heart. Right? Even if something lightly brushes your eyebrows, the heart reacts. When a fly lands, the heart feels it. 
In this way, we don’t know where our heart is, but is it close to us or far? It’s close. Even in the darkest night, if you try to do something bad, the heart says, "You rascal!" Isn’t that right? "Yes." So it’s the closest, but we don’t know where that heart is. It feels as if it’s not there. Why? Because it’s too close. Did your eyes come into being to see things that are far away or to see things that are close? You can only see what is within a certain range. If you bring something too close, can you see it? Even if it’s there, you can’t see it. 
Why is that? Because the eyes were created to see the other. The eyes are designed to relate to the other and see them centered around where the other is, so they cannot see beyond that range. Everything is like that. 
You definitely want to make the most precious thing yours, right? "Yes." Therefore, to make God your God, your heart must be that big. Your heart must be large enough to accommodate God. 
But how is your heart? If God enters, will it be full or lacking? Will your heart’s desires be enough? They are big, right? "Yes." If there are ten Gods, would you want to make all ten your God or not? "I would want to." So your heart is that big, isn’t it? "Yes." Your heart is big enough to welcome God. That’s how big the heart is. 
However, if it’s narrow, it’s very narrow. It’s so narrow that you can’t even breathe or smell anything. When it’s wide, it’s infinitely wide, and when it’s narrow, it’s infinitely narrow. So when does it become wide and when does it become narrow? If there’s something better, it can become as wide as it wants. Even if you have made this world yours, if there’s something better than the world, would you want to abandon the world and have that? "I would want to." You want that. 
Ultimately, if God is the absolute being of the universe and the most precious being, then He must be captured in the human heart. The heart can expand infinitely for something better and contract infinitely for something worse. Do you understand? 
There are many women here, and it might be rude to say this, but I can’t help it. Are women’s hearts wide or narrow? "Narrow." You acknowledge that. (laughter) So when it’s narrow, it’s narrow, but when it’s wide, how is it? Does it lose to men? "No." (laughter) That’s how it is. When women’s hearts are narrow, they must be blocked; otherwise, everything would leak out. Isn’t that right? "Yes." 
The criteria for determining good and bad 
A heart that is too good and has no beginning or end is useless anywhere. (laughter) You need to understand this. You shouldn’t like this and that. Of course, it’s welcome to like something better, but you shouldn’t like everything indiscriminately. You shouldn’t abandon the good position you have reached to pursue something lower. However, seeking something slightly better is always welcome. 
When does sadness arise? Sadness arises when you fall from a good position to a bad position. Then what is something better? It is to rise to a better position. You need to understand this. 
So what determines good and bad? It is determined by whether you get closer or further from the absolute being who possesses the highest value. If you take even one step closer to Him, you become happier and more joyful; if you take even one step away, you become worse and sadder. In this way, human joy and sorrow are determined based on the absolute Lord. The scales of joy and sorrow for us humans go back and forth centered on the absolute Lord. 
When we look at our ladies, their hearts are narrow, but they can discern good from bad well. That’s what women are like. Men may have wide hearts, but there are pitfalls. They like this and that. However, women are different. If it’s this, it’s this; if it’s that, it’s that; they don’t like both. That’s why it fits perfectly when you match a woman to the bottom of a man who is not sharp. You just need to match them perfectly. So men and women are meant to work together. 
You want to make the best thing yours, but it would be a big problem to display it outwardly. The more precious it is, the more you want to keep it deep inside, in your very bones. Isn’t that right? "Yes." Does anyone walk around saying, "I have a diamond worth several carats here, come and see!"? Women, the more precious something is, the more they think, "Oh, there are many thieves…," and even if they put it in their wallets, they don’t trust it and carry it on their waist or in their chest, covering it with their hands as they walk. (laughter) Even then, they can’t feel at ease, thinking, "Oh, it would be great to hide it deep in my bones, but I can’t do that, what should I do?" They even sleep holding it. Why is that? There is a desire in everyone to hide the most precious things deeply where no one knows. The more precious it is, the more they want to bury it deep. Do you understand? "Yes." 
They discuss it with it, relate to it, laugh with it, and live praising it; such a person is a happy person. How wonderful would that be? 
The most precious things are kept in the deepest, secret marrow. Isn’t that a nice saying? The less valuable something is, the more it is displayed outwardly. Isn’t that right? "Yes." Then where should the highest value in the universe, God, be kept? What if He were placed in this human world where human thieves live? People would fight over God, risking their nations and the world. So it’s good that we don’t know where God is. (laughter) Think about it. 
It is fortunate that God exists as an invisible being. 
In Cape Town, South Africa, there is currently a significant issue centered around diamond production. Similarly, if humans were to find out where God is, all the powerful people would fight to make God their own. If that were to happen, there would probably be thousands of years of conflict over God. So God has thought very wisely. It is very reasonable for God to make Himself invisible. (laughter) It couldn’t be any other way. 
Only the owner knows. Only those who possess the secret can know. Only His sons and daughters know. If you knew that, would you feel good or bad? "Good." If you knew that, even if you wandered around with empty hands, you would feel good, and even if you missed a meal, it wouldn’t matter. Even if you couldn’t sleep for a night, that wouldn’t be a problem. Just thinking about it feels good, doesn’t it? Wouldn’t it? Even if others are making a fuss about your death, you would say, "If I die, then let it be." (laughter) 
In the future, the name of Reverend Moon of the Unification Church will keep coming up. However, I hope for that time and will work to make it happen. Does that make you feel bad? "No, it feels good." Even if it makes you feel bad, there’s nothing you can do about it. So what happens if we apply such a law centered on God? Since God Himself is a precious universal being, when humans come to know God, great things happen. The world goes into chaos all at once. Everyone, do you know about the recent crowd crush incident in England? There was a soccer match, and many people gathered to watch it, resulting in a crowd crush as reported in the newspapers, right? The meeting point of heavenly principles and human morality
